<br />

Idk, but it smells spicy to my nose. I can't shake while wearing this. It makes it not to great when it is super hot outside. <br />
its 505/50, being fresh and clean, which is what I would have preferred more of. <br />

I think I will try the new reformulated bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2318918"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2318918#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318805" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I can confirm, Profondo edp 2024 has been modified slightly- and it is less screechy. <br />

DNA-wise, It's still Profondo 2020 but it's less salty and green. Improtant to note: I also find it to be a lot, lot, weaker than my bottles of original Profondo 2020. It lasts a while but it sits close. Profondo 2020 was one where if you put your nose up close it felt like a big blast of dense aromachemicals, whereas 2024 isn't a punch to the face.<br />

this is actually my everyday (i own the 2024 EDP reformulation). this was the first fragrance that i bought and i love it. although it's pretty generic smelling, like most blue fragrances, i feel like this takes the best qualities of each blue fragrance on the market and mixes them together to create this beast. one caveat, at least for me, is that smelling this on myself for a prolonged period of time makes me sick of it. i've read that a lot of people find this boring and generic, which i can agree with to an extent because this is a blue fragrance after all.<br />
<br />
<br />
the longevity is good, on skin it lasts 6-7 hours before becoming a skin scent. on clothes it lasts for a week. the sillage and projection is good, not obnoxious or intoxicating if sprayed correctly. this projects fairly well even towards the 6th hour mark. this is a great fragrance that (i believe) you can't go wrong with at all. maybe you can find better for the price, but imo this is a solid choice and you can't go wrong with it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It's a scent you can wear anywhere, anytime. Because of this, it may come across as 'common', 'standard' or even 'boring', but it has an edge which makes it distinguishable. When sprayed on the skin, the scent is a bit too similar to Chrome Extreme for me, though when sprayed on clothes, the scent is truly a delight, blue yet marine as well, masculine and classy like few others. Longevity and projection are not that great though, 2-3 hours max.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2283345"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2283345#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2283160" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It does a great job painting a marine, sea salty feeling around you. Doesn’t offensively project, and is a nice dumb reach for spring summer. Reminds me a bit of Millesime Imperial with better performance.<br />

Opening hits you with the classic citrus airyness you’d expect from ADG with that added element of aquatic sea saltiness, and it’s not too much either it’s just the right balance. Performance is 4-6 hours at best.<br />
<br />
My only knock with this is the ADG line as a whole runs together so similarly that if you have any version of Profondo, Parfum, or original, you’re set. You do not need to own multiple.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1983639">HBeez</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 19:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Love this stuff! <br />
<br />
Yes, it isn't the most unique or shocking scent but it's a very well done and blended masculine fragrance. The marine notes are beautiful and well complimented by a sharp slightly bitter and green notes (probably the cypress?). It smells clean and soapy, maybe due to the lavender, so it might give a bit of a shower gel vibe. <br />
<br />
Ideally a summer scent for daytime casual use, but very versitile and works for the office and gym. Ideal age is 25+, as it's on the mature side, but can be pulled off 20+.<br />
<br />
Performance is below average and you have to compensate by overapplying, but I've seen worse.<br />
<br />
Overall great stuff, if only they made it more concentrated.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2260014"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2260014#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2258758" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173048">Dvmaak</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 15:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I like this, but I don't love it.<br />
The smell is immediately recognizable as an AdG scent. Yes, there are differences, but to the average person, it's 95% similar to the OG AdG, which has been used by the vast majority of population for decades. I say this because just the other day, I experienced this myself... <br />
<br />
I bough myself a brand new bottle AdG Profondo at full retail at the nearby Macy's. After doing far more research than I care to admit on which flanker to buy, I decided on Profondo. It seemed the freshest, the most modern, the most refined out of the others. To be honest, I loved the idea of smelling like a mineral note; like a hardened man who just got done mining near the sea. Wow...<br />
<br />
Rushing home to show my girlfriend my new purchase, her first words are "this smells like my uncle".<br />
To clarify, she hasn't seen her uncle in 10+ years as he has been DEAD, but we can all relate to the memory of a scent. She associated this scent to her uncle because he probably work the OG AdG. In fact, most people have probably already worn the OG AdG at some point in their lives. It's not unique, it's not going to stun anyone, it smells like a million other guys, but the smell is pleasant!.<br />
<br />
8/10<br />
<br />
For what it's worth, the new 2024 bottle performs great on my skin. I can genuinely smell it after a 9 hour workday.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2258758"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2258758#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2251498" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I think it smells great, but you must smell it on your skin. This is one of those fragrances that smells very different on skin compared to a paper strip. It smells okay, but boring when you smell the sprayer or smell it on paper, but on warm skin it really comes alive and pops!<br />
<br />
Very clean, fresh, like a bright blue sky. It's a great summer fragrance, especially if, like me, you tend to favor cold weather fragrances and have trouble finding something to wear when it's hot.<br />

Scent: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 7/10<br />
Projection: 6/10<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2226714" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="rombass"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/212984"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.212984.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="rombass" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2226714ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2226714" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/212984">rombass</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-23">07/23/24 01:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just can't help loving this fragrance. If you don't, don't read on. Lots of good words to follow :)<br />
<br />
I can't remember what the original Acqua di Gio smells like, it's been maybe 15 years since I last smelled it, but this flanker is so addictive. You don't always need a red carpet, special event perfume to make a bold statement. Armani know what they are doing. All the criticism about this being a "been there, done that" scent is laughable.<br />
<br />
This is a scent you can wear pretty much anywhere, anytime, and people will remember that you smell nice, and that's often the point. Much better than being remembered for smelling disgusting after wearing my Rasasis, which contain precious aged Indian farts like Oud. I know I smelled unique when I wore them and definitely made a bold and incredibly awful statement and some of the people I used to be with when I wore those perfumes, I am no longer with<br />
<br />
Anyway, Profondo reminded me a bit of Versace Pour Homme / Chanel Allure Sport. For a freshie, it's quite long-lasting with a moderate but noticeable projection.<br />
<br />
I'm not saying my heavy amber and patchouli scents are useless, but I think this Armani freshie has a place in everyone's collection. It would probably fit in where you would choose to wear Bleu de Chanel, or similar type of scent.<br />
<br />
I can see myself wearing this when I want to go out with friends and be happy, it's a happy scent, easy going, likeable, soft in nature, not a motorbike rider with tough talk bragging about picking up 50 chicks on the way from nowhere to nowhere.<br />
<br />
I've noticed that people often criticise these types of scent for being "just another aquatic/blue/marine" fragrance, as if it were something inferior. I am even more surprised to hear this from YT reviewers, some of whom I respect. They criticise a fragrance because it doesn't stand out, because it's simple, because it's been done a hundred billion times before, but maybe their lives aren't so repetitive and they live each day in a completely different way to the day before. They must be outstandingly fun to be with, right? I'd like to know what they are remembered for then...</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2226714"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2226714#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2223285" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The sky is cloudy and everything is drowning in the visceral beating of the waves hitting the cliff and boulders. <br />
It is to me A Coruña, Spain or some mystical place in Oregon. Not quite sure but something of the sort. :3</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2193768"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2193768#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2191241" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Projection 4/10. <br />

"Rounder", less edgy.<br />
Fragheads that love character in a fragrance will not like the changes-but these changes are made with the average person in mind.<br />
Profondo 2024 is an even safer fragrance and the quintessential dumb reach for warm weather. <br />
Totally inoffensive and very likeable. Perfect for the office.<br />
You WILL smell great to others. Forgettable, but great.<br />
People who want an ADG signature scent should stick with (now discontinued) Profumo/Profondo Lights and the OG Profondo.<br />
<br />
Profondo 2024 is an NPC's fragrance-but one that excels at that.<br />
3/10 for originality<br />
9/10 for smell<br />
10/10 for achieving it's intended role<br />
<br />
My brand new bottle performs just as well as the older version-so longevity should be somewhat better when the juice macerates.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; You do realise Profondo EDP was reformulated in 2024 (along with the whole ADG line - new bottle gradient and sizes) and it now lasts longer and projects better?<br />
<br />
People commenting that it doesn't last long probably don't even know about the reformulations that have happened.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2185614"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2185614#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2185393" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2176791" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BaroqueBookwyrm"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1494447"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1494447.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="BaroqueBookwyrm" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Armaf/Club-de-Nuit-Precieux-93272.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.93272.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Club de Nuit Precieux"title="Club de Nuit Precieux"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2176791ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2176791" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1494447">BaroqueBookwyrm</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-03">06/03/24 11:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I received this fragrance for free when it was sent to me in error. I purchased a fragrance for my wife for mother's day and this came instead. It's the big 4.2oz bottle, so a nearly $200 value for free. I mainly wear clone fragrances out of protest for the ridiculous markup on designer and niche fragrances, so when I say that I wouldn't purchase this fragrance on purpose, you can take that with a grain of salt.<br />
<br />
I've worn this a few times since I got it. Off the top you get bergamot and an erbacious rush of lavender and rosemary along with the marine notes that are the raison d'être of this flanker. My nose doesnt detect any mandarin, but my nose isn't the most precise instrument on this forum. Feels very green-blue in the opening. In the drydown it becomes a pleasant blue fragrance, losing most of its fougere character in exchange for amber and mineral notes. The moss remains throughout though, so it can be considered a blue-green fragrance instead a simple blue. <br />
<br />
I sprayed it on the back of my wrist, elbow of my shirt, and behind my ear at 7:00 AM. It is now 12:30 and though I have gone noseblind to it, one of the ladies in my office reports that she can smell it, that she likes it, and that it isn't too strong. I'll update this review when I get home from work and see if my wife can detect it beyond intimate distances. The sillage is undetectable to my nose, and I can really only get whiffs of it when directly smelling my wrist.<br />
<br />
Update: can be smelled at arms reach. Pretty good performance overall.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is a portrait of a sailboat captain. He wears linen shirts that may as well not have buttons for how often he wears them open to the wind and spray, but he has the abs to pull it off even though he isn't a young guy. He has the barest hint of salt in his five-o-clock shadow to complement the seawater that pumps in his veins. He is quiet, and a bit pretentious. His feet know the sway of a deck and his hands are filled with the knowledge of a thousand knots. He's the kind of guy who has mermaid stories and you cant tell if he's just messing with you, if he's crazy, or if he knows something you don't. His other boat is a yacht, but he prefers sailing on the open seas with canvas and rope. He is easy to respect, but hard to like.<br />
<br />
In comparison to Azzaro Chrome Extreme, my clone for this fragrance, the opening is entirely different. The Chrome is lacking any fougere character besides the moss and screeches a bit with more metallic minerals right off the bat. It's more silver-blue in the opening in contrast the the green-blue of ADG Profondo. In the drydown they align much closer, although the ADG is a bit sweeter, more wearable, approachable, and office safe, where the Azzaro is a bit more challenging. The ADG has a higher quality smell to it in the drydown but, If I remember correctly, the Azzaro was louder for longer, or perhaps isn't as susceptible to olfactory fatigue.<br />
<br />
Correction: I wore ADG on the right and Azzaro on the left today. On my skin, ADG Profondo is stronger for longer. It has three distinct stages where it starts fougere, moves into a hybrid of a blue and a fougere, and drys down as a blue. At all stages it is louder than the Azzaro. The Azzaro is linear, never changing from the opening except to lose a bit of citrus off the top, but it always remains pleasant. It is sweeter and not nearly as metallic as I remember. It is not bolder or more challenging, it is softer and more office safe than the ADG. Honestly, I can hardly call Chrome Extreme a clone of ADG Profondo at this point. They share marine notes and a mossy saltiness, but not much else. Perhaps my bottle of Chrome Extreme has changed due to maceration (its like 3 years old at this point), or perhaps my memory for fragrances isn't as good as I thought. Either way, this free ADG will remain in my collection as a summer weekend staple.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2176791"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2176791#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176586" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2140752" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="valeri0706"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/396740"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.396740.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="valeri0706" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Y-Eau-de-Parfum-50757.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.50757.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Y Eau de Parfum"title="Y Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2140752ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2140752" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/396740">valeri0706</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-30">04/30/24 00:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>@mohammed_r37<br />
<br />
The new 2024 bottle of the OG EDT lasts very long - around 6-7 hours. It also smells citrusy and fresh.<br />
<br />
However, both Profondo EDP and Parfum smell more modern and refined. Profondo has that ozonic, mineralic undertone and it is amazing in high heat. If you've never tried the EDT, it smells the simplest of them all, but still amazing. I mean, it's a best-seller for a reason.<br />
<br />
However, I believe Parfum smells best. It is the reincarnation of Profumo (now discontinued), which used to be my favourite fragrance of all time and a signature for a few years for a long time. It smells herbal and has incense. It's perfect for any occasion, even in colder months.<br />
<br />
You can't really go wrong with any of them, but I'd recommend testing Parfum if you can. And whatever you do, make sure to get the 2024 bottle with the GA engraving placed at the very bottom. Both the new and old bottles are on Armani's UK website (Armani Beauty), if you want to make a visual comparison. <br />
<br />
The 2024 bottles of all 3 "main" players of the ADG line (EDT, Profondo &amp; Parfum) just smell fresher and last longer than the old bottles.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2139912"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2139912#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2139784" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2139784" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JusttheFactsMan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1733487.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JusttheFactsMan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Montale/Infinity-81773.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81773.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Infinity"title="Infinity"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2139784ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2139784" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-29">04/29/24 06:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#658 in my "Tour de Fragrance"<br />
<br />
I wore ADG EDT while dating someone that preferred it, but I was never happy with the scent's performance (or the relationship). I honestly have had equivalent performance from $7 Cuba Paris scents.  So I stopped wearing it in favor of the Armani Code EDT when I moved on from that relationship. I did kinda like the breezy beach character of ADG, so thought maybe it would do better with an EDP. So I tried again with ADG Profumo. The performance was once again at the level of a cologne, so I gave it away, and was not at all surprised when it was discontinued. But hope springs eternal and I got a sprayette of Profondo out of curiosity and in response to the hype surrounding every fragrance this L'Oreal unit puts out, and again, there is absolutely nothing profound about Profondo. If I had been blindfolded when I first smelled it I would have said it was Missoni Wave, which costs less than half what this costs for 100ml. <br />
<br />
I have every Tommy Bahama freshie, and all are beach wear like this ADG scent, and they perform at least a well as this 5X more expensive fragrance. I agree it smells okay in the opening, but there's nothing thereafter. It's a short-lived and barely projecting scent. And before you accuse me of anosmia, my friends at breakfast all avowed they couldn't smell anything, and I all but bathed in this stuff only an hour before. I reapplied it at lunch and met a girlfriend for coffee and desert at 3. She couldn't smell it without smelling nose to skin. So it isn't just me.<br />
<br />
L'Oreal's "Giorgio Armani" fragrances benefit from name association with the clothing designer and brand. The clothing design house has unique &amp; personality-based designing for the high end market tier. The best in the world according to some. And as in all of these fashion designer-branded fragrances, they have nothing whatever to do with the L'Oreal-owned and operated fragrance brand that is a 100% mass-market, low-tier, non-premium fragrance brand that has nothing in common with the Giorgio Armani design house and certainly does not share their philosophy. But thanks to that name association and the great marketing surrounding it, L'Oreal gets positive buzz for otherwise mediocre and undifferentiated mass consumer fragrances carrying the Armani name. Eventually mediocrity catches up with every product, just as mediocrity caught up with Profumo, and it will eventually catch up with this fragrance as well.<br />
<br />
Lattafa's "Liam Blue Shine" is the same scent as this for $22. I threw it away after first use, but if you like Profumo, you'll recognize it in that Lattafa scent. Same with Azzaro's $30 Chrome Extreme which is at least in a less ugly bottle than the Liam Blue. And the aforementioned Missoni Wave costs $40. You can pay $100 plus for a designer name if you like, but you can do SO much better than this with virtually any Mancera blue or marine scent, all of which perform better than ADG Profondo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1227835">blaqice</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-10">04/10/24 11:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm in a love-hate relationship with this fragrance. The opening has a smell that I can't quite put my finger on. The best way I can describe it is you're at the beach on a extremely hot, humid day, and all of a sudden there's a thunderstorm with heavy rain, but only for about 30 minutes. Then the sun comes out, there is not a cloud in the sky and you start to get wafts of the smell of the sun drying the rocks and the wet ground. That smell, mixed with the citrus and the newly created ozone from the lightning is the best way I can describe what I'm smelling in the opening. Now these notes on their own are fine, but for some reason when they combine they sort of have this musty, slightly sweaty "gym bag" kind of smell as someone described it below. I'm not sure what is causing this for me, possibly the mineral notes combined with the aquozone. I have never been one of those people who has a sensitivity to these aquatic scents. I don't smell any fishy/weird smells in any other AdG, or even Light Blue Eau Intense.<br />
<br />
I noticed that this odd smell I get is more pronounced AFTER I take a shower and then spray this. If I spray this on later in the day or during a day that is particularly hot and humid, and I am slightly more sweaty than I would usually be, I don't notice this odd smell as much, so maybe people who naturally have more sweaty/oily skin won't notice this as much (I do have particularly dry skin). I also don't get this odd smell at all when I spray on clothes, so it definitely must be a skin chemistry thing.<br />
<br />
As this dries down, though, it does smell really good. The lavender and cypress combined with the aquatic notes smells pretty amazing and I think the rating here on Fragrantica is totally justified. Longevity and projection are about the same that I get with the EdP, maybe slightly less, but not as good as the AdG Parfum. If I didn't get this weird smell for around the first hour, this would easily be a love for me, but as of right now it's a strong like. More so than any other AdG, I would advise that you test this on skin first, and if you try it first in cool weather, or an air-conditioned office and don't like it, try it again on a hot, humid day or a day where you will be outdoors more.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I love the fruity, citrus in the opening that gives this a touch of sweetness  . As it dries down the lavender adds warmth along with the fresh , spicy accords . Also this is slightly herbal, with a beautiful, clean musk. I reach for this often especially in the warmer months however it can be pulled off all year around, definitely a very versatile, fresh fragrance. Personally I get great performance from this one, it projects like crazy for three hours on my skin and I can smell it lingering all day, which is always enjoyable. You can get a 4.2 oz bottle on eBay as well as discounters for well under $100 which is well worth the money in my opinion. As soon as my bottle empties, I will get another because this is a must have in my collection. Aquatic fragrances are nothing new but ADG is the first one to do it and this one is very well done . <br />
 <br />
9/10<br />

And since it’s not the newest release from Aqua di Gio line, can be found at such affordable prices nowadays!<br />
<br />
As far as a classic designer masculine perfume goes, there is not much that gets close to Profondo  for me. Speaking from the perspective of smelling this on a man during hot season! Aqua di Gio Profondo and Hermes Eau Givree are my most favourite scent to smell on my husband in hot  and humid weather!<br />
<br />
This flanker is in my opinion the best of Aqua di Gio  line. It’s strong but not overwhelming, it’s marine and warm in the same time, balsamic and fresh spicy, with aromatic, citrusy touches, a tad of fruity sweetness and some woods in the deep dry down. It’s long lasting, 8 hours plus on my husband, and projects well for about two hours! It’s summertime at seaside bottled! <br />
<br />
I have heard on YT that the 2020 version might be discontinued and a new Profondo Parfum is available in 2024. I will have to check on Armani Website and if that’s the case, I have to get a back up bottle for my husband’s collection (and my  pleasure of smelling this on him continuously in the near future)! <br />
<br />
This is Alberto Morillas (and Italian perfumery) at its finest! I really hope that this is not discounted as I have heard…</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="2093429"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=2093429#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2088395" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2084013" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="john49494"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1998081"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="john49494" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2084013ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2084013" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1998081">john49494</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-06">03/06/24 07:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Acqua di Gio Profondo is a fragrance that has captivated many enthusiasts since its release. Created by renowned perfumer Alberto Morillas for Giorgio Armani, it's an olfactory journey that embodies depth, sophistication, and the essence of the sea. Let's delve into a comprehensive review of this iconic scent.<br />
<br />
Presentation:<br />
The presentation of Acqua di Gio Profondo is sleek and elegant, reflecting the luxuriousness of the Armani brand. The bottle design is reminiscent of a polished sea stone, with deep blue hues that evoke the depths of the ocean. The simplicity of the design is striking, with the fragrance name etched in bold lettering, conveying a sense of strength and masculinity.<br />
<br />
Fragrance Notes:<br />
Acqua di Gio Profondo opens with a refreshing burst of marine notes, immediately transporting you to the crisp, invigorating waters of the Mediterranean. The top notes are a harmonious blend of aquatic accords, bergamot, and green mandarin, creating an initial impression that is vibrant and energetic.<br />
<br />
As the fragrance settles, the heart notes emerge, revealing a captivating blend of cypress, lavender, and rosemary. These herbal elements add a touch of aromatic complexity to the composition, evoking the rugged beauty of coastal landscapes. The scent feels effortlessly masculine, yet refined and sophisticated.<br />
<br />
In the dry down, Acqua di Gio Profondo reveals its depth and sensuality with a base of mineral amber, patchouli, and musk. These warm, earthy notes lend a lingering richness to the fragrance, leaving a lasting impression that is both alluring and comforting.<br />
<br />
Longevity and Projection:<br />
One of the standout features of Acqua di Gio Profondo is its impressive longevity and projection. Despite its fresh and aquatic character, the scent has remarkable staying power, lingering on the skin for hours without becoming overpowering. It strikes a perfect balance between presence and subtlety, making it suitable for both daytime and evening wear.<br />
<br />
Versatility:<br />
Acqua di Gio Profondo is a versatile fragrance that can be worn in a variety of settings and seasons. Its refreshing aquatic notes make it perfect for summer days spent by the sea, while its underlying depth and complexity make it equally suitable for formal occasions or romantic evenings. Whether you're heading to the office, attending a social event, or simply relaxing with friends, this fragrance is sure to make a lasting impression.<br />
<br />
Overall Impression:<br />
In conclusion, Acqua di Gio Profondo is a modern classic that embodies the spirit of adventure, sophistication, and masculinity. Its evocative blend of marine, herbal, and woody notes creates a multi-dimensional olfactory experience that is both refreshing and alluring. From its elegant presentation to its long-lasting performance, every aspect of this fragrance speaks to the impeccable craftsmanship and attention to detail for which Giorgio Armani is renowned. Whether you're a longtime fan of the Acqua di Gio line or discovering it for the first time, Acqua di Gio Profondo is sure to leave a lasting impression.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792">Atomikbomb_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-22">02/22/24 19:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's literally a surf fest, but in the BEST way!<br />
<br />
Yes, this is blue as hell, I agree entirely, but it's a really quenching, pleasant, satisfying blue fragrance. My husband has a sample of this and we both really enjoy it.<br />
<br />
The citrusy opening is awesome! It's lots of tart citrus without being too fruity or annoying, nothing cloying or overkill here, but it's refreshing. I disagree with people saying it smells like alcohol, to me personally it levels out within 5 seconds (anything can be an alcohol bomb if you sniff it before 5 seconds).<br />
<br />
It doesn't really develop into much in terms of herbal notes, but there is something mildly green underneath the blue...all of it remains a very background tone though.<br />
<br />
Ultimately, it's 80% marine-y and it definitely has some salt, but it doesn't come off as bitter or briney. No, longevity isn't stellar, but it's a freshie and I've certainly experienced much more fleeting aquatic male fragrances that left my man and I wondering why anyone would pay for something that lasts only 20 minutes. This stays around for about 4 hours.<br />
<br />
At any rate, this is a great male fragrance (yes, I'm a chick but I review absolutely anything I can or feel like), and I think it would be perfect in hot weather, both in terms of performance and for it's cooling qualities.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;     <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Positive Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1245567" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1245567" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Bfreepro417"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1195501"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1195501.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Bfreepro417" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Oud-Noir-17338.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.17338.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Versace Pour Homme Oud Noir"title="Versace Pour Homme Oud Noir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1245567ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1245567" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1195501">Bfreepro417</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-11-06">11/06/20 18:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Beautiful fragrance, really a treat for someone like me who grew up enjoying the original. I’ve always had a soft spot for fresh, aquatic scents, and the AdG EDT was my signature scent for many, many years in high school and beyond. I still have a bottle, but obviously I’ve grown and tastes change, and I tend to prefer scents with a bit more depth and density these days. <br />
<br />
I tried this and profumo the same day, one on each wrist. I love them both, but this one truly surprised me, especially because so many more people recommended Profumo. <br />
<br />
The opening is heavenly. If you like the original, trust me, you will LOVE this. It’s taken that sparkly, citrusy, aquatic airiness of the original and amped it up, slightly more of a marine vibe, and it is much more grown up. The marine notes, the citrusy florals, absolute freshness with a slight warmth to it... beautiful, truly a treat to behold. You can really tell the increased quality and are given a much richer, deeper, and denser fragrance. Surprisingly versatile too, I’m one of the few people who really enjoy wearing fresh fragrances all year round instead of wearing something sweeter and warmer in the winter. There are some that just wouldn’t hold up, but this one really does well in all weather and settings. It’s youthful and bright but also deep and sophisticated, a really nice balance in my opinion: it doesn’t smell like you’re some rich guy in a tuxedo who drives a rolls Royce, it smells more like someone who craves adventure, sensuality, and subtle luxury in equal measures. <br />
<br />
The opening is my favorite part of this fragrance, but I do greatly enjoy it through all stages. The drydown is where it differs most from Profumo, it’s more of a mineral/aquatic vibe throughout, not as warm. <br />
<br />
I’ve noticed some comparisons with polo blue and “blue” frags like BdC or sauvage, and I can see how this is a valid comparison, but I find it also does this fragrance a disservice. Yes it’s a more aquatic version of the original, but I feel it does not try to be a “blue” fragrance (like BdC, sauvage, Dylan blue, Luna Rossa carbon, etc). If you do not like fragrances like those, don’t write this one off, it’s not in the same ballpark! There is an entirely different structure to the fragrance and it blends every note together almost flawlessly: freshness, sweetness, florals, spice, it’s almost perfectly blended. Not flat and boring or overly synthetic and harsh. Much more lively, sparkling, and more tolerable in large doses than the “blue” frags. <br />
<br />
Longevity and projection are both fantastic. At least 8 hours on skin and multiple hours of solid projection depending on temperature. <br />
<br />
9/10. I love it!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="1245567"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=1245567#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1195740" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; As a fragrance, Profondo splits the difference between the depth of ADG profumo (minus the incense) and the cypress/rosemary forward verdancy of L'Eau Bleue d'Issey (the dry down), all three kind of living in the same olfactory ballpark as the original ADG.  It's nice and I suppose it has its place if you don't own either of the two -- but then you could probably own both for the price of a single bottle of this stuff.  So it's both a "like" and a pass for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="59532"comment_id="1263595"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profondo-59532.html?ccid=1263595#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1150170" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1150170" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mrpoopybutthole"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1220080"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1220080.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="mrpoopybutthole" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Eau-de-Parfum-71606.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.71606.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Acqua di Giò Eau de Parfum"title="Acqua di Giò Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1150170ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1150170" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);
